		<category name="Gemstone E-Tech and Special Weapons">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Enables Gemstone variants of E-Techs to spawn, as well as Gemstone versions of Unique/Legendary/Seraph items (at increasingly lower rates) that appear in the base game or Tiny Tina DLC (no other DLC, for legal reasons and such).</comment>
				<comment>Options to toggle what and what does not spawn are available, such as preventing E-Techs but allowing Special weapons, or preventing special weapons that are normally elementally locked like the Thunderball Fists from spawning as Gemstones (on by Default). You can further toggle each of those by manufacturer/gem (Quartz, emerald, etc.).</comment>
				<comment>NOTES;</comment>
				<comment>Guns that are not included in the main game or Dragon's Keep DLC are not included. This is due to the game deleting the gun barrel upon entering a save file, and I can't legally fix that.</comment>
				<comment>The game will delete the weapons if you do not run the mod before loading a save file.</comment>
				<comment>These operate in the same way Hyperion Diamond E-Tech Pistols do, meaning they can spawn with no element, or accessories that otherwise wouldn't be present on the normal, non-Gemstone version (or may be missing them, like the Law's blade).</comment>
				<comment>Run this after the Jakobs & Torgue E-Techs mod or disable the Gemstone lines, if you use it.</comment>
				<comment>If you use the option in "Jakobs & Torgue E-Techs" to enable Torgue Blasters to have explosions, be sure to turn on one of the fixes so that Rock Blasters and Emerald Blasters spawn with the appropiate barrel.</comment>
				<comment>Due to hotfix "brilliance", Aquamarine Railers won't work unless you do the following;</comment>
				<comment>1. Load up a file that doesn't have the Aquamarine Railer, and start up a game.</comment>
				<comment>2. Activate this mod.</comment>
				<comment>3. Exit back to main menu.</comment>
				<comment>4. Activate this mod.</comment>
				<comment>5. Load the file with the Aquamarine Railer on it.</comment>
			</category>
